. ** Exercise 1
. 
. set seed 1
{txt}
{com}. set obs 10000 
{txt}{p}
number of observations (_N)  was 0,
now 10,000
{p_end}

{com}. gen X1 = runiform(1, 3) 
{txt}
{com}. gen X2 = rgamma(3, 2)
{txt}
{com}. gen X3 = rbinomial(1, 0.3)
{txt}
{com}. gen eps = rnormal(2, 1)
{txt}
{com}. 
. gen Y = 0.5 + 1.2 * X1 - 0.9 * X2 + 0.1 * X3 + eps
{txt}
{com}. egen Y_mean = mean(Y)
{txt}
{com}. gen ydum = (Y > Y_mean)
{txt}
{com}. 
. ** Exercise 2
.

{txt}
{com}. *** Correlation is 0.2036. This quantity is different from 1.2.
